</div></div><script>
(function(){
    function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
        var d = new Date();
        d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
        var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();
        document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires + ";path=/";
    }
    function getCookie(cname) {
        var name = cname + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = decodeURIComponent(ca[i]);
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
                c = c.substring(1);
            }
            if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
                return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
            }
        }
        return "";
    }

    var cookieName = "wt_mc_shop_mediacode_intern";
    var invalidChar = 'ü';

    if(window.cookieStore === undefined) {
        var wt_mc_shop_mediacode_intern = getCookie(cookieName);
        if (wt_mc_shop_mediacode_intern !== "" && wt_mc_shop_mediacode_intern.includes(invalidChar) > -1 ) {
            setCookie(cookieName, encodeURIComponent(wt_mc_shop_mediacode_intern), 30);
        }

    } else {
        window.cookieStore.get(cookieName).then(cookie => {
            if(cookie && cookie.value && cookie.value.indexOf(invalidChar) > -1) {
                window.cookieStore.set({
                    name: cookieName,
                    value: encodeURIComponent(cookie.value),
                    expires: cookie.expires,
                    domain: cookie.domain,
                });
            }
        });
    }
})();
